position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; max-inline-size: 488px; padding: 12px 8px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row; padding: 0px 8px;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">does github recognize both as license</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span>Yes,&nbsp;</span><span><a rel="noopener" href="https://github.com/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">GitHub</a></span>&nbsp;</span><span style="font-weight: 700;">recognizes both</span>&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE.md</code>&nbsp;as valid license files for your repository.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 94.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub Docs</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">GitHub</span>&nbsp;uses an open-source tool called&nbsp;</span><span style="font-weight: 700;">Licensee</span>&nbsp;to detect these files in the root of your project. It specifically looks for a variety of common naming patterns, including:<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.5391px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+2</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">LICENSE</span>&nbsp;(the most common and default choice)</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">LICENSE.md</span>&nbsp;(parsed and displayed as Markdown)</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">LICENSE.txt</span>&nbsp;(treated as plain text)</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">COPYING</span>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">COPYING.md</span></span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 96.375px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub Docs</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+6</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Key Recognition Rules</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Location Matters</span>: The file must be in the&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">root directory</span>&nbsp;of your repository to be automatically identified in the "About" section on the right sidebar.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Case Sensitivity</span>: While generally flexible, the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://docs.github.com/en/communities/setting-up-your-project-for-healthy-contributions/adding-a-license-to-a-repository" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">GitHub documentation</a></span>&nbsp;suggests using&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">all caps</span>&nbsp;(e.g.,&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE.md</code>) to ensure reliable detection.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Content Detection</span>: For GitHub to display a specific license name (like "MIT" or "Apache 2.0") instead of just "Other," the content of the file must match a standard template with about&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">90% similarity</span>.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Precedence</span>: If you have both&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE</code>&nbsp;and&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE.md</code>&nbsp;in your root folder, GitHub typically defaults to&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE</code>&nbsp;and may ignore the Markdown version for API and UI identification.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 109.438px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Stack Overflow</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+5</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like help choosing a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">standard license template</span><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">&nbsp;to ensure&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">GitHub</span>&nbsp;displays the correct metadata for your project?</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>Yes, GitHub also recognizes&nbsp;</span><span style="font-weight: 700;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING</code></span>&nbsp;(or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING.md</code>) as a valid license file.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 66.1797px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GitHub</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">While it functions exactly like a&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE</code>&nbsp;file for GitHub’s detection metadata, it carries a specific historical "vibe":<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">GNU Tradition</span>: The use of&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING</code>&nbsp;is a convention strongly associated with&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">GNU and FSF projects</span>&nbsp;(like the GPL or LGPL).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Dual-File Setup</span>: Some larger projects use&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">both</span>:</span><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING</code>: contains the full, verbatim legal text of a standard license (like the GPLv3).</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: circle; padding-inline-start: 0px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">LICENSE</code>: contains project-specific notices, copyright years, or mentions of third-party dependencies.</span></li></ul></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Technical Detection</span>: GitHub's automated system specifically looks for names like&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING</code>&nbsp;or&nbsp;<code dir="ltr" style="line-height: 22px; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border: 1px solid var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 4px; padding-block: 2px; padding-inline: 4px;">COPYING.md</code>&nbsp;in your root directory to identify your project's license.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 67.7188px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; min-height: var(--aim-container-min-height); color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; max-inline-size: 488px; padding: 12px 8px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row; padding: 0px 8px;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">what does copyleft or copyright mean</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>In simple terms,&nbsp;</span><mark style="border-radius: 4px; background-image: ; background-position-x: ; background-position-y: ; background-size: ; background-repeat: ; background-attachment: ; background-origin: ; background-clip: ; padding: 0px 2px;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">copyright</span>&nbsp;is the default legal protection that gives you exclusive control over your work, while&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">copyleft</span>&nbsp;is a specific way of using that law to ensure your work (and any improvements to it) stays open and free for everyone</mark>.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 109.93px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GeeksforGeeks</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Copyright: "All Rights Reserved"</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Copyright is the standard legal framework that automatically applies to an original work as soon as it is created.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 97.4844px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Safe Creative</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Ownership</span>: You own the exclusive right to copy, distribute, or modify your work.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Restriction</span>: No one else can use, sell, or change your work without your explicit permission or a license.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Goal</span>: Protects the creator's financial interests and total control over their intellectual property.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 112.039px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">GeeksforGeeks</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Copyleft: "All Rights Reversed"</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Copyleft is a clever play on words and a specific type of license that uses copyright law to enforce sharing rather than restriction.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 97.4844px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Safe Creative</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Mandatory Sharing</span>: Anyone who receives your work can use, modify, and redistribute it, but&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">only</span>&nbsp;if they also use the exact same copyleft terms for their version.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">"Viral" Nature</span>: If someone adds a feature to your copyleft code, they must release that new code under the same license—they cannot turn it into a private, proprietary product.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Goal</span>: Ensures that a project remains in the public domain and that all future improvements benefit the entire community forever.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 80.8203px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Wikipedia</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+3</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Quick Comparison</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div style="overflow-x: auto; margin-block: 16px 24px; box-sizing: border-box; scrollbar-width: none; inline-size: calc(100% + 20px); padding-inline-end: 24px;"><table style="border: none; border-collapse: collapse; table-layout: auto; width: 648px;"><tbody><tr><th height: 108.375px;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; flex-direction: column; flex: 1 1 0%; position: relative; min-block-size: 0px; min-inline-size: 0px;"><div style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.4; margin: 0px 0px 4px; color: var(--jINu6c); display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden;"><span>Creative Commons, Copyleft, and Other Licenses - Copyright ...</span></div><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); margin: 0px 0px 8px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.3; display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden;">Jan 28, 2026 —&nbsp;<span>Copyleft. ​Copyleft, a play on the word "copyright," is the practice of offering users of a work the right to freely distribute an...</span></span><div style="align-items: center; align-self: flex-end; display: flex; width: 242px; margin-right: auto; margin-block-end: 8px; margin-top: auto;"><div style="display: flex; border-radius: 50%; align-items: center; justify-content: center; width: fit-content; vertical-align: middle;"><div style="width: 16px; height: 16px; line-height: 16px; display: flex; flex-shrink: 0; align-items: center; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--EoKObe); border-radius: 50%;"></div></div><div style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; text-wrap: nowrap; color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; flex-direction: column; margin-inline-start: 8px;"><span style="align-items: center; position: relative; display: flex; justify-content: center; align-items: center; cursor: pointer; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"><svg fill="currentColor" height="18px" viewBox="0 -960 960 960" width="18px"><path d="M480-160q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-240q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-320q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-240q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-160Zm0-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-480q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-560q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-480q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-400Zm0-240q-33 0-56.5-23.5T400-720q0-33 23.5-56.5T480-800q33 0 56.5 23.5T560-720q0 33-23.5 56.5T480-640Z"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div style="border-radius: 8px; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></body></html>

---

<html><head></head><body><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: auto ease 0s 1 normal none running none; padding-top: 30px; position: relative; opacity: 1; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; max-inline-size: 488px; padding: 12px 8px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row; padding: 0px 8px;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">how is opensource license respected in reality</span></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>In reality, open-source licenses are respected through a combination of&nbsp;</span><span style="font-weight: 700;">legal necessity</span>,&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">corporate policy</span>, and&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">community norms</span>. While the code is free to download, failing to follow its license terms—such as&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://gunnercooke.com/when-free-isnt-free-the-hidden-risks-of-open-source-licensing/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">attribution or sharing derivative code</a></span>—can lead to copyright infringement.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 129.625px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Palo Alto Networks</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. Legal and Business Enforcement<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Open-source licenses are&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://finitestate.io/blog/open-source-license-compliance" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">legally binding agreements</a></span>, and courts have established that violating them is a form of copyright infringement.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 87.4688px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Finite State</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Due Diligence:</span>&nbsp;Major compliance checks often happen during&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">M&amp;A transactions, IPOs, or funding rounds</span>. Investors and buyers use audits to ensure there are no "hidden" legal risks from improperly used code.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Copyright Litigation:</span>&nbsp;While rare compared to proprietary lawsuits, copyright holders (like individual developers or foundations) can sue for damages or force companies to&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.paloaltonetworks.com/blog/cloud-security/why-you-need-proactive-open-source-license-compliance/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">release their proprietary code</a></span>&nbsp;as open-source if they violate "copyleft" licenses.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Internal Policies:</span>&nbsp;Large companies often use automated tools like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.leanix.net/en/wiki/trm/open-source-licenses" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">Software Bill of Materials (SBOM)</a></span>&nbsp;and license scanners to track dependencies and ensure they don't accidentally ship code under incompatible licenses.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 65.3594px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Reddit</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+6</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. Community and Social Pressure<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Beyond the law, the "respect" for licenses is often maintained by the developers themselves.<span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Reputation Risk:</span>&nbsp;Publicly violating a license can lead to severe&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=8hbkfKAl4hk" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">community backlash</a></span>&nbsp;and damage a brand's reputation among the talent pool it needs to hire.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The "Microscope" Effect:</span>&nbsp;Popular projects have thousands of eyes on them. This public scrutiny pressures companies to follow best practices and contribute back, as they may face&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://openmetal.io/resources/blog/is-open-source-software-secure/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">widespread criticism</a></span>&nbsp;if they exploit volunteer labor without honoring the terms.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 76.1016px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">YouTube</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+4</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. Practical Limitations<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Despite these mechanisms, respect is not universal:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Enforcement Gaps:</span>&nbsp;Open-source software lacks automatic enforcement; it is often just a text file in a repository. Smaller maintainers often lack the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://arxiv.org/html/2503.02817v2" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">financial resources to sue</a></span>&nbsp;large corporations for violations.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">SaaS Loophole:</span>&nbsp;Many standard licenses (like GPLv2) only trigger obligations when code is "distributed." Companies providing software as a service (SaaS) can often&nbsp;<span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;">use and modify code internally</span>&nbsp;without sharing changes, which led to the creation of the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://opensource.com/article/17/9/open-source-licensing" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">AGPL license</a></span>&nbsp;to close this gap.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Ethics vs. Law:</span>&nbsp;Most open-source licenses do not restrict&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">who</em>&nbsp;can use the software or for what purpose. Developers who don't want their work used for things like&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.reddit.com/r/linux/comments/1ix3imu/ethical_open_license_eol_a_different_take_on_open/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">mass surveillance</a></span>&nbsp;often find their "open" license prevents them from legally stopping such use.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 75.7734px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">YouTube</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+5</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Would you like to see a&nbsp;<span style="font-weight: 700;">comparison table</span>&nbsp;of the most common open-source licenses and their specific requirements?<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div><div style="clear: both; display: flex; flex-flow: wrap; row-gap: 16px; margin-block: 18px 0px; justify-content: space-between;"><div style="display: contents;"></div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; flex-shrink: 1; width: 652px; align-items: center;"><div style="display: flex;"><div style="position: relative; display: inline-flex;"><span style="inline-size: 20px; block-size: 20px;"><div><svg fill="currentColor" width="20px" height="20px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" margin: 0px 16px;"></div></li><li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><div style="padding-block: 12px 4px; padding-inline: 20px; position: relative; overflow: hidden;"><a rel="noopener" href="https://finitestate.io/blog/open-source-license-compliance#:~:text=Common%20misunderstandings%20about%20open%20source,Identifying%20open%20source%20components" style="text-decoration-line: none; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); position: absolute; inset: 2px; z-index: 1; outline: 0px;"></a><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; justify-content: center; gap: 8px; height: 108.375px;"><div style="box-sizing: border-box; display: flex; flex-direction: column; flex: 1 1 0%; position: relative; min-block-size: 0px; min-inline-size: 0px;"><div style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 1.4; margin: 0px 0px 4px; color: var(--jINu6c); display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden;"><span>All You Need to Know About Open Source License Compliance</span></div><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); margin: 0px 0px 8px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.3; display: -webkit-box; -webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; overflow: hidden;">Sep 5, 2024 —&nbsp;<span>All You Need to Know About Open Source License Compliance. Discover common misconceptions about open-source licenses and learn bes...</span></span><div style="align-items: center; align-self: flex-end; display: flex; width: 242px; margin-right: auto; margin-block-end: 8px; flex: 0 0 82px; width: var(--thumbnail-width); height: 82px; overflow: hidden; position: relative; margin-block-end: 8px; --thumbnail-width: 82px;"></div></div></div></li></ul><div style="position: relative; padding: 4px 20px 16px;"><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: stretch; border-radius: 9999px; color: var(--jINu6c); cursor: pointer; display: flex; justify-content: center; overflow: hidden; position: relative; background-color: var(--aYn2S); outline: 0px;"><span style="font-size: 14px; line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div style="--fade-in-animation: fade-in-new-response 150ms cubic-bezier(0.3,0,0.8,0.15); animation: var(--fade-in-animation); padding-top: 30px; position: relative; margin-top: 24px; color: rgb(230, 232, 240); font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 14px; white-space-collapse: collapse; background-color: rgb(16, 18, 24);"><div style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 10px; max-width: 652px; z-index: 1; margin-top: 0px;"><div><div style="display: flex; gap: 4px; margin-left: auto; width: fit-content;"><div style="display: flex; position: relative; overflow: hidden; background-color: var(--XKMDxc); border-radius: 24px 4px 24px 24px; width: fit-content; flex-direction: column; gap: 12px; max-inline-size: 488px; padding: 12px 8px; margin-left: auto;"><div style="display: flex; flex-direction: row; padding: 0px 8px;"><span role="heading" style="-webkit-box-orient: vertical; -webkit-line-clamp: 2; display: -webkit-box; overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; overflow-wrap: break-word; font-size: 16px; line-height: 24px; white-space-collapse: preserve;">i feel it's already to a great extent impossible even before the llm era. llms make it even easier. and techinically you could not really control after you open something.</span><div role="button" tabindex="0" style="align-items: center; height: fit-content; margin-left: 8px; margin-top: auto; display: flex; flex: 1 1 auto; place-content: end; outline: 0px;"><div style="color: rgb(139, 140, 145); height: 14px; margin-bottom: 2px; rotate: 180deg; width: 14px;"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 12 7" width="14px" fill="none"><path d="M6.00046 0.166733C5.88929 0.166733 5.78654 0.184733 5.69221 0.220733C5.59771 0.256899 5.50604 0.3194 5.41721 0.408234L0.583711 5.24173C0.422711 5.40273 0.340795 5.59573 0.337962 5.82073C0.335128 6.04573 0.417045 6.24157 0.583711 6.40823C0.744878 6.5694 0.939379 6.64998 1.16721 6.64998C1.39488 6.64998 1.5893 6.5694 1.75046 6.40823L6.00046 2.16673L10.2505 6.40823C10.4116 6.5694 10.6047 6.6514 10.8297 6.65423C11.0547 6.6569 11.2505 6.5749 11.4172 6.40823C11.5782 6.24723 11.6587 6.05282 11.6587 5.82498C11.6587 5.59715 11.5782 5.40273 11.4172 5.24173L6.58371 0.408234C6.49488 0.3194 6.40321 0.256899 6.30871 0.220733C6.21438 0.184733 6.11163 0.166733 6.00046 0.166733Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></div></div></div></div></div><div style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: flex; font-size: 12px; justify-content: end; line-height: 16px;"></div><div></div></div></div><div><div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div style="color: var(--m3c11,#eef0ff); position: relative; --m3c9: #e6e8f0; --m3c11: #e6e8f0; display: flex;"><div style="width: 652.438px;"><div><div style="display: contents;"></div></div><div dir="ltr" style="width: 652px; max-width: var(--CYi3c--fRcLaf,652px);"><div style="display: contents;"><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);"><span>You are touching on the "untraceability" problem that has plagued open source for decades, which LLMs have indeed accelerated.</span><span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">1. The "Pre-LLM" Reality: Trust over Tracking<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Even before AI, you are correct that once code is released, technical control is lost.<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Honors System:</span>&nbsp;Most open-source compliance relied on the&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://finitestate.io/blog/open-source-license-compliance" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">honors system</a></span>. Small developers couldn't possibly monitor every private repository in every corporation to see if their GPL code was being used.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Reactive vs. Proactive:</span>&nbsp;Enforcement was almost entirely reactive. It only happened if a company became successful enough to be audited during an IPO or if a developer happened to recognize their unique variable names or bugs in a competitor’s product.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><div style="align-items: center; display: flex; gap: 4px; height: 14px; overflow: hidden; width: 84.4766px;"><span style="font-family: &quot;Google Sans&quot;, Roboto, Arial, sans-serif; color: var(--IXoxUe); font-size: 11px; line-height: 1.45; display: flex; overflow: hidden; min-width: 0px;"><span style="overflow: hidden; text-overflow: ellipsis; min-width: 0px;">Bird &amp; Bird</span><span style="flex-shrink: 0;">&nbsp;+1</span></span></div></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">2. The LLM Era: "License Washing"<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">LLMs introduce what many call "license washing," making enforcement exponentially harder:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Loss of Lineage:</span>&nbsp;Traditional compliance tools look for matching code "fingerprints." LLMs, however, don't copy-paste; they learn patterns and&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://arxiv.org/html/2408.02487v1" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">re-generate code</a></span>. This breaks the chain of attribution, making it nearly impossible to prove that a specific line of code came from a specific licensed project.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Fair Use Defense:</span>&nbsp;Many AI companies argue that training models on licensed code is&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.arl.org/blog/training-generative-ai-models-on-copyrighted-works-is-fair-use/" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">fair use</a></span>&nbsp;because the model is "transformative." If courts agree, the license terms (like requiring attribution) may become legally irrelevant during the training phase.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">The Verbatim Risk:</span>&nbsp;The only remaining "control" occurs when a model spits out code&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://blog.genlaw.org/CameraReady/57.pdf" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">verbatim</a></span>. If an LLM reproduces a complex, unique function from a GPL project without attribution, the user—and potentially the AI provider—could still be liable for&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://arxiv.org/html/2403.15230v1" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">copyright infringement</a></span>.</span><span><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span>&nbsp;</span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></li></ul><div></div><div role="heading" style="margin-block: 24px 12px; font-family: var(--Aoh9Xe); font-size: var(--qpdFp); font-weight: var(--JT4IPc); line-height: var(--qYGXw); letter-spacing: 0px; color: var(--jINu6c);">3. The Shift in Control<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><div style="font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; overflow-wrap: break-word; margin-block: var(--xdqYEb--pNrv5d,12px) var(--xdqYEb--i8AQde,16px);">Because technical control is impossible once code is "open," the community is shifting its strategy:<span style="visibility: hidden;"><span style="position: relative; text-wrap: nowrap;"><span></span><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); display: inline-block; transform: rotate(135deg);"><svg style="margin-top: 3px;" fill="currentColor" width="12px" height="12px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path d="M3.9 12c0-1.71 1.39-3.1 3.1-3.1h4V7H7c-2.76 0-5 2.24-5 5s2.24 5 5 5h4v-1.9H7c-1.71 0-3.1-1.39-3.1-3.1zM8 13h8v-2H8v2zm9-6h-4v1.9h4c1.71 0 3.1 1.39 3.1 3.1s-1.39 3.1-3.1 3.1h-4V17h4c2.76 0 5-2.24 5-5s-2.24-5-5-5z"></path></svg></span></span></span></div><ul style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-block: 12px 16px; font-family: var(--nkmQOe); font-size: var(--z3BFIe); font-weight: var(--XWliwc); line-height: var(--a9X0Jc); letter-spacing: 0px; padding-inline-start: 16px;"><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Poisoning the Well:</span>&nbsp;Some developers are experimenting with "data poisoning" or&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://law.stackexchange.com/questions/102317/is-there-an-open-source-software-license-restricting-ai-model-training" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">anti-AI licenses</a></span>, though these are often legally untested or technically easy to bypass.</span></li><li style="margin: 0px 0px 12px; padding: 0px; list-style: disc; padding-inline-start: 4px;"><span style="overflow-wrap: break-word;"><span style="font-weight: 700;">Automated Audits:</span>&nbsp;Companies are now using AI-powered "license scanners" to catch code that&nbsp;<em style="font-weight: inherit;">feels</em>&nbsp;like it might be from a restricted library, moving from "exact match" searching to&nbsp;<span><a rel="noopener" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PutO8IZV3xw" style="text-decoration-thickness: 1px; text-decoration-color: var(--JKqx2); -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1); text-underline-offset: 1px; outline: 0px;">probabilistic detection</a></span>.</span><span><span style="position: relative; hidden;"><span>Paradoxical feeling of using AI for open source code, worrying about ...</span></div><span style="color: var(--IXoxUe); margin: 0px 0px 8px; font-size: 12px; line-height: 1.3; display: line-height: 20px; margin: 8px 16px;">Show all</span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div><div></div></div></div></div><div
